 ---------------------- 
User : What does bhagavad gita say about other religions
AI : Your question touches on a broader aspect of faith. The Bhagavad Gita (18.66) emphasizes surrendering to the divine will rather than adhering to rigid doctrines. Krishna does not denounce any faith but advocates for righteousness (dharma) and devotion (bhakti). Other religious texts also convey similar messages of truth and compassion. Guidance: Recognize that all religions aim to elevate humanity. Interfaith dialogue and understanding can foster peace and harmony. Avoid divisive interpretations and focus on shared values like love, justice, and wisdom.

sarva eva hi.' Meaning: Krishna assures that those who seek Him, irrespective of their paths, reach Him. Guidance: The Gita emphasizes that all sincere paths lead to the divine truth. Different religions are various expressions of the same spiritual quest. The essence of faith is devotion and righteousness, regardless of external rituals. Guidance: The Bhagavad Gita acknowledges and respects the diversity of spiritual paths, confirming that truth transcends religious boundaries. It emphasizes that devotion, faith, and righteous living are key to spiritual realization. In today's context, this teaches us to appreciate different religions as unique expressions of the same universal truth, promoting interfaith harmony.
